PART III - LANDS  
 
Title Registration 
 
REGISTRATION  OF  TITLE ACT, No.  21 OF  1998  
 
Declaration  of  Determination  of  the  Commissioner  of  Title  Settlement  under  Section  14 
 
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under Section 14 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998, I, the undersigned, hereby de-
clare my determination as set out in the Schedule appended hereto in regard to the  title to parcel of Land Nos. 132 of Block 02, con-
tained in the Cadastral Map No. 320238, situated in the Village of Kotakedeniya, within the Grama Niladhari Division of No. 46 - 
Palkumbura in the Divisional Secretary's Division of Udunuwara, in the District of Kandy, in the Province of Central, referred to in 
Notice No. 32/0151 calling for claims to land parcels which was duly published in the Gazette  No. 1579/08 of 08th December, 2008 in 
terms of Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998. 
 
 
 K.A.K. RANJITH  DHARMAPALA , 
 Commissioner of Title Settlement. 
 
Land Title Settlement Department, 
No. 1200/6, â€œMihikatha Meduraâ€, 
Rajamalwatta Road, 
Battaramulla. 
18th August, 2016.

BY virtue of the powers vested in me under Section 14 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998, I, the undersigned, hereby de-
clare my determination as set out in the Schedule appended hereto in regard to the  title to parcel of Land Nos. 10, 15, 31, 58, 88, 90, 95, 
117, 137 and 141 of Block 01, contained in the Cadastral Map No. 320272, situated in the Village of Ambagasthenna, within the Grama 
Niladhari Division of No. 68 - Ambagasthenna in the Divisional Secretary's Division of Udunuwara, in the District of Kandy, in the 
Province of Central, referred to in Notice No. 32/0279 calling for claims to land parcels which was duly published in the Gazette  No. 
1667/8 of 08th November, 2010 in terms of Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998.
